mkdir iso/ || echo ""

xorriso -as mkisofs -b limine-cd.bin \
-no-emul-boot -boot-load-size 4 -boot-info-table \
--efi-boot limine-eltorito-efi.bin -efi-boot-part \
--efi-boot-image --protective-msdos-label iso -o MoonOS.iso 
limine/limine-install MoonOS.iso 
qemu-system-x86_64 -M q35 -cpu qemu64 -m 1G -serial stdio -no-reboot -smp 4 -no-shutdown -cdrom MoonOS.iso  -enable-kvm -cpu host -cpu qemu64,+la57 -bios /usr/share/ovmf/OVMF.fd
